<td align="left" style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Results of Operation and Financial Condition. </p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">On July&#160;29, 2024, ON Semiconductor Corporation announced in a news release its financial performance for the second quarter ended June&#160;28, 2024 and other related material information (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Earnings Release</span></span>&#8221;). A copy of the Earnings Release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and incorporated herein by reference. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">The information in Item&#160;2.02 of this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</span> including Exhibit 99.1, is being furnished under Item&#160;2.02 and shall not be deemed to be &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight:bold"><span style="font-style:italic">Exchange Act</span></span>&#8221;), or otherwise subject to liability under that section, nor shall such information be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, regardless of any general incorporation language in such filing, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:36pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:18pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>onsemi Announces Second Quarter 2024 Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Free cash flow increase of ~$250&nbsp;million year over year </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:30pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>SCOTTSDALE, Ariz., &#150; July</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;29, 2024 &#150;</B> onsemi (the &#147;Company&#148;) (Nasdaq: ON) today announced results for the second
quarter of 2024 with the following highlights: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Revenue of $1,735.2&nbsp;million </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:4pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">GAAP gross margin and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> gross margin of 45.2% and 45.3%,
respectively </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:4pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">GAAP operating margin and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating margin of 22.4% and
27.5%, respectively </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:4pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">GAAP diluted earnings per share and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per
share of $0.78 and $0.96, respectively </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:4pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="10%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="justify" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Returned ~$650&nbsp;million of free cash flow over last twelve months to shareholders through stock
repurchases </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We remain dedicated to driving growth through market share gains, doubling down on investments in strategic markets,
and expanding the breadth of our portfolio of industry-leading products with analog and mixed-signal solutions,&#148; said Hassane <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">El-Khoury,</FONT> president and CEO, onsemi. &#147;As reflected by our recent supply
agreement with Volkswagen Group, we also continue to strengthen our silicon carbide leadership position in automotive as we ramp production with leading global OEMs in Europe, North America and China.&#148; </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="justify">Diluted shares outstanding can vary as a result of, among other things, the vesting of restricted stock
units, the incremental dilutive shares from the convertible notes, and the repurchase or the issuance of stock or convertible notes or the sale of treasury shares. In periods when the quarterly average stock price per share exceeds $52.97 for the 0%
Notes, and $103.87 for the 0.50% Notes, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted share count and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> net income per share include the anti-dilutive impact of the hedge transactions
entered concurrently with the 0% Notes, and the 0.50% Notes, respectively. At an average stock price per share between $52.97 and $74.34 for the 0% Notes, and $103.87 and $156.78 for the 0.50% Notes, the hedging activity offsets the potentially
dilutive effect of the 0% Notes, and the 0.50% Notes, respectively. In periods when the quarterly average stock price exceeds $74.34 for the 0% Notes, and $156.78 for the 0.50% Notes, the dilutive impact of the warrants issued concurrently with such
notes is included in the diluted shares outstanding. GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted share counts are based on either the previous quarter&#146;s average stock price or the stock price as of the last day of the
previous quarter, whichever is higher. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

impairments and other, net; goodwill impairment charges; gains and losses on debt prepayment; actuarial (gains) losses on pension plans and other pension benefits; and certain other special items, as necessary. These special items are out of our
control and could change significantly from period to period. As a result, we are not able to reasonably estimate and separately present the individual impact or probable significance of these special items, and we are similarly unable to provide a
reconciliation of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. The reconciliation that is unavailable would include a forward-looking income statement, balance sheet and statement of cash flows in accordance with GAAP.&nbsp;For
this reason, we use a projected range of the aggregate amount of special items in order to calculate our projected <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating expense outlook. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

additional way of viewing aspects of our operations that, when taken together with GAAP results and the reconciliations to corresponding GAAP financial measures that we also provide in our releases, provide a more complete understanding of factors
and trends affecting our business. Because <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are not standardized, it may not be possible to compare these financial measures with other companies&#146;

(Nasdaq: ON) is driving disruptive innovations to help build a better future. With a focus on automotive and industrial <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">end-markets,</FONT> the company is accelerating change in megatrends such as vehicle
electrification and safety, sustainable energy grids, industrial automation, and 5G and cloud infrastructure. <B>onsemi</B> offers a highly differentiated and innovative product portfolio, delivering intelligent power and sensing technologies that
solve the world&#146;s most complex challenges and leads the way to creating a safer, cleaner, and smarter world. <B>onsemi </B>is recognized as a Fortune 500<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> company and included in the <FONT

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:14pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">To supplement the consolidated financial results prepared in accordance with GAAP, onsemi uses
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">certain&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,</FONT> which are adjusted from the most directly comparable GAAP measures to exclude items related to the amortization of acquisition-related intangibles, expensing of appraised
inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,&nbsp;inventory</FONT> valuation <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">adjustments,&nbsp;in-process&nbsp;research</FONT> and development expenses, restructuring, asset impairments
and other, net, goodwill impairment charges, gains and losses on debt <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">prepayment,&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;interest</FONT> expense, actuarial (gains) losses on pension plans and other pension benefits, third party
acquisition and divestiture-related costs, tax impact of these items and certain other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> items, as necessary. Management does not consider the effects of these items in evaluating the core
operational activities of onsemi. Management uses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> internally to make strategic decisions, forecast future results and evaluate onsemi&#146;s current performance. In addition,
the Company believes that most analysts covering onsemi use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> to evaluate onsemi&#146;s performance. Given management&#146;s and other relevant parties&#146; use of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures,</FONT> onsemi believes these measures are important to investors in understanding onsemi&#146;s current and future operating results as seen through the eyes of management. In addition,
management believes <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> are useful to investors in enabling them to better assess changes in onsemi&#146;s core business across different time periods. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">These&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> are not prepared in accordance with, and should not be considered alternatives or necessarily superior to, GAAP financial data and may be different
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">from&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;measures</FONT> used by other companies. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Because&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures are not standardized, it may not be possible to compare these
financial measures with other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">companies&#146;&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measures, even if they have similar names. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Revenue </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> revenue allows management to evaluate, among other things, the revenue from the
Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent of special items. In addition, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-</FONT> GAAP revenue is an important component of management&#146;s
internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future
results. Management presents this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate the Company&#146;s revenue generation performance relative to the direct costs of operations of
onsemi&#146;s core businesses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Gross</FONT> Profit and Gross Margin </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;gross</FONT> profit and gross margin allows management to evaluate, among other
things, the gross margin and gross profit of the Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT> including, generally
speaking, expensing of appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,</FONT> impact of business wind down and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> facility costs. In addition, it is an important
component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining
targets and forecasting future results. Management presents <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">this&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate our operating performance independent of certain <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items and the effects of certain variables unrelated to our overall operating performance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Operating</FONT> Income and&nbsp;Operating Margin </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;operating</FONT> income and operating margin allows management to evaluate, among other things, the operating margin and operating income of the Company&#146;s core businesses and trends across
different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT> including, generally speaking, expensing of appraised inventory fair market
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,</FONT> impact of business wind down, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> facility costs,&nbsp;amortization and impairments of intangible assets, third party acquisition and
divestiture-related costs, restructuring charges and certain other special items as necessary. In addition, it is an important component of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess
the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future results. Management presents
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">this&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT> measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate our operating performance independent of certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items and the effects of
certain variables unrelated to our overall operating performance. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">10 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> MEASURES (Continued) </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="font-size:14pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP&nbsp;Net</FONT> Income Attributable to ON Semiconductor
Corporation and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Diluted Earnings Per Share </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;net</FONT> income attributable to onsemi and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per share allows management to evaluate the operating results of onsemi&#146;s core
businesses and trends across different reporting periods on a consistent basis, independent <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;non-cash&nbsp;items</FONT> including, generally, the amortization and impairments of intangible assets, expensing of
appraised inventory fair market <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">value&nbsp;step-up,</FONT> impact of business wind down, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> facility costs, restructuring, gains and losses on debt prepayment,
actuarial (gains) losses on pension plans and other pension benefits, third party acquisition and divestiture-related costs, discrete tax items and other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> tax adjustments and certain other special
items, as necessary. In addition, these measures are important components of management&#146;s internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process, as they are used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business
and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, setting targets and forecasting future results. For our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> reporting, we are utilizing a projected and normalized
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> effective tax rate of 16%. We calculate this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> effective tax rate on an annual basis. We expect to use this normalized
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> effective tax rate of 16% through 2025, however, we may update this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> effective tax rate at any time for a variety of reasons, including, but not limited
to, the rapidly evolving global tax environment, significant changes in our geographic earnings mix or changes to our strategy or business operations. Management presents <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">these&nbsp;non-GAAP&nbsp;financial</FONT>
measures to enable investors and analysts to understand the results of operations of onsemi&#146;s core businesses and, to the extent comparable, to compare our results of operations on a more consistent basis against those of other companies in our
industry. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Free Cash Flow </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use
of free cash flow allows management to evaluate, among other things, the ability of the Company to make interest or principal payments on its debt. Free cash flow is defined as the difference between cash flow from operating activities and capital
expenditures disclosed under investing activities in the consolidated statement of cash flows. Free cash flow is not an alternative to cash flow from operating activities as a measure of liquidity. It is an important component of management&#146;s
internal performance measurement and incentive and reward process as it is used to assess the current and historical financial results of the business and for strategic decision making, preparing budgets, obtaining targets and forecasting future
results. Management presents this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure to enable investors and analysts to evaluate our financial performance independent of the cash capital expenditures. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Diluted Share Count </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="justify">The use of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted share count allows management to evaluate, among other things, the
potential dilution due to the outstanding restricted stock units excluding the dilution from the convertible notes that is covered by hedging activity up to a certain threshold. In periods when the quarterly average stock price per share exceeds
$52.97 for the 0% Notes and $103.87 for the 0.50% Notes, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted share count includes the anti-dilutive impact of the Company&#146;s hedge transactions issued concurrently with the 0% Notes and
the 0.50% Notes, respectively. At an average stock price per share between $52.97 and $74.34 for the 0% Notes and $103.87 and $156.78 for the 0.50% Notes, the hedging activity offsets the potentially dilutive effect of the 0% Notes and the 0.50%
Notes, respectively. In periods when the quarterly average stock price exceeds $74.34 for the 0% Notes and $156.78 for the 0.50% Notes, the dilutive impact of the warrants issued concurrently with such notes are included in the diluted shares
outstanding. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

</DIV></Center>
